at Hull, 28 October 2016</li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other">Other</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Scotland_national_rugby_league_team&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Other">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>Biggest home attendance: 2,233 vs France at Glasgow, 9 July 1997</li>\n<li>Biggest away attendance: 21,009 vs England at Coventry, 5 November 2016</li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Scotland_A">Scotland A</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Scotland_national_rugby_league_team&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Scotland A">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Scotland_A_national_rugby_league_team" title="Scotland A national rugby league team">Scotland A national rugby league team</a></div>\n<p>The Scotland A national rugby league team nicknamed the <b>Bravehearts</b> is made up of amateur players, who either play in the <a href="/wiki/Rugby_League_Conference" title="Rugby League Conference">Rugby League Conference</a> the BUCS university league or the Scottish domestic competition.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Napier_University" class="mw-redirect" title="Napier University">Napier University</a> has also played a huge part in the team, with many Napier students having played in the side over the years.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup> The team regularly compete against England, Wales and Ireland, playing them annually in the <a href="/wiki/Skanska_Amateur_Four_Nations" title="Skanska Amateur Four Nations">Skanska Amateur Four Nations</a>. Since the creation of this tournament, in 2002, Scotland have won it just once in 2010. In 2003 Scotland embarked on a mini tour of Europe playing in <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a>, <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Serbia" title="Serbia">Serbia</a>, helping expand rugby league in those country by playing domestic and national sides.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup> Former player and winner in 2010 <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mike_Wallace(rugby_league)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Mike Wallace(rugby league) (page does not exist)">Mike Wallace</a> currently coaches the side.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Match_officials">Match officials</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Scotland_national_rugby_league_team&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Match officials">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<ul><li>Referees: <a href="/w/index.php?title=Gary_Owram&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Gary Owram (page does not exist)">Gary Owram</a> and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Gordan_Wallace&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Gordan Wallace (page does not exist)">Gordan Wallace</a></li>\n<li>Touch judges: <a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_Rudd_(RLEF)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Kevin Rudd (RLEF) (page does not exist)">Kevin Rudd (RLEF)</a></li>\n<li>Match Commissioner: <a href="/w/index.php?title=Ian_McGregor_(SL)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Ian McGregor (SL) (page does not exist)">Ian McGregor (SL)</a></li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a
